! *** Black ***
! This is a light-on-dark tileset, so our first and most important
! color is black.  We define several blacks for various needs:

! Entirely transparent background:
BB = (0, 0, 0, 0)
! Standard opaque black background:
Bb = (0, 0, 0)
! Just _almost_ bright enough to be visible against the above:
Bc = (48,48,48)
! That, but 50% transparent (useful for shadows):
Bd = (48,48,48,127)
! Another shade brighter (black monsters, use this):
Be = (72,72,72)
! Medium brightness:
Bf = (127,127,127)

! Now, then, some real colors.  For each hue, we define
! the following color variants:
! b - lightest, off-white (most brandings use this)
! c - saturated pastel (most monsters use this)
! d - saturated pastel, 50% transparent (unsolids, etc.)
! e - desaturated, not as light as the pastel (most items use this)
! f - medium brightness (used e.g. by walls)
! g - dark (only used in terrains)

! *** Red (hue 0) ***
Cb = (255, 220, 220)
Cc = (255, 174, 174)
Cd = (255, 174, 174, 127)
Ce = (174, 124, 124)
Cf = (144, 56, 56)
Cg = (64, 0, 0)

! *** Orange (hue 21) ***
Db = (255, 227, 212)
Dc = (255, 202, 174)
Dd = (255, 202, 174, 127)
! *** Brown ***
De = (174, 142, 124)
Df = (144, 87, 56)
Dg = (64, 22, 0)

! *** Gold (hue 48) ***
Eb = (255, 246, 212)
Ec = (255, 239, 174)
Ed = (255, 239, 174, 127)
! *** Ochre ***
Ee = (174, 164, 124)
Ef = (144, 126, 56)
Eg = (64, 51, 0)

! *** Spring Green (hue 72) ***
Fb = (248, 255, 220)
Fc = (239, 255, 174)
Fd = (239, 255, 174, 127)
Fe = (164, 174, 124)
Ff = (126, 144, 56)
Fg = (56, 64, 0)

! *** Teal Green (hue 156) ***
Gb = (220, 255, 241)
Gc = (174, 255, 223)
Gd = (174, 255, 223, 127)
Ge = (124, 174, 154)
Gf = (56, 144, 109)
Gg = (0, 64, 38)

! *** Baby Blue (hue 198) ***
Hb = (220, 244, 255)
Hc = (174, 231, 255)
Hd = (174, 231, 255, 127)
He = (124, 159, 174)
Hf = (56, 118, 144)
Hg = (0, 45, 64)

! *** Indigo (hue 255) ***
Ib = (229, 220, 255)
Ic = (194, 174, 255)
Id = (194, 174, 255, 127)
Ie = (137, 124, 174)
If = (78, 56, 144)
Ig = (16, 0, 64)

! *** Violet (hue 280) ***
Jb = (243, 220, 255)
Jc = (228, 174, 255)
Jd = (228, 174, 255, 127)
Je = (157, 124, 174)
Jf = (115, 56, 144)
Jg = (43, 0, 64)

! *** Magenta (hue 312) ***
Kb = (255, 220, 248)
Kc = (255, 174, 239)
Kd = (255, 174, 239, 127)
Ke = (174, 124, 164)
Kf = (144, 56, 126)
Kg = (64, 0, 51)

! *** White ***
Ob = (255, 255, 255)
Oc = (248, 248, 248)
Od = (248, 248, 248, 127)
Oe = (200, 200, 200)
Of = (176, 176, 176)
! If you need darker than that, see Bf under blacks, above.
